\DoxyCodeLine{539 DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \textcolor{keyword}{extern} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} is\_running\_in\_test;}
\DoxyCodeLine{540 }
\DoxyCodeLine{541 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{542 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE unsigned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{543 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{544 }
\DoxyCodeLine{545 \textcolor{comment}{// A 24 byte string class (can be as small as 17 for x64 and 13 for x86) that can hold strings with length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{546 \textcolor{comment}{// of up to 23 chars on the stack before going on the heap -\/ the last byte of the buffer is used for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{547 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ "{}is small"{} bit -\/ the highest bit -\/ if "{}0"{} then it is small -\/ otherwise its "{}1"{} (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{548 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ capacity left before going on the heap -\/ using the lowest 5 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{549 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ 2 bits are left unused -\/ the second and third highest ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{550 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ acts as a null terminator if strlen() is 23 (24 including the null terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{551 \textcolor{comment}{//              and the "{}is small"{} bit remains "{}0"{} ("{}as well as the capacity left"{}) so its OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{552 \textcolor{comment}{// Idea taken from this lecture about the string implementation of facebook/folly -\/ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{553 \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{554 \textcolor{comment}{// TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{555 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ optimizations -\/ like not deleting memory unnecessarily in operator= and etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{556 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ resize/reserve/clear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{557 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{558 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ back/front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{559 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ iterator stuff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{560 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ find \& friends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{561 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ push\_back/pop\_back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{562 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ assign/insert/erase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{563 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ relational operators as free functions -\/ taking const char* as one of the params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{564 \textcolor{keyword}{class }DOCTEST\_INTERFACE String}
\DoxyCodeLine{565 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{566 \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{567     \textcolor{keyword}{using }size\_type = DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE;}
\DoxyCodeLine{568 }
\DoxyCodeLine{569 \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{570     \textcolor{keyword}{static} DOCTEST\_CONSTEXPR size\_type len  = 24;      }
\DoxyCodeLine{571     \textcolor{keyword}{static} DOCTEST\_CONSTEXPR size\_type last = len -\/ 1; }
\DoxyCodeLine{572 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1065 String toString() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1066 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if DOCTEST\_MSVC >= 0 \&\& DOCTEST\_CLANG == 0 \&\& DOCTEST\_GCC == 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1067     String ret = \_\_FUNCSIG\_\_; \textcolor{comment}{// class doctest::String \_\_cdecl doctest::toString<TYPE>(void)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1068     String::size\_type beginPos = ret.find(\textcolor{charliteral}{'<'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1069     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret.substr(beginPos + 1, ret.size() -\/ beginPos -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}String::size\_type\textcolor{keyword}{>}(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}>(void)"{}})));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1070 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1071     String ret = \_\_PRETTY\_FUNCTION\_\_; \textcolor{comment}{// doctest::String toString() [with T = TYPE]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1072     String::size\_type begin = ret.find(\textcolor{charliteral}{'='}) + 2;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1324 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1325 \textcolor{comment}{// This will check if there is any way it could find a operator like member or friend and uses it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1326 \textcolor{comment}{// If not it doesn't find the operator or if the operator at global scope is defined after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1327 \textcolor{comment}{// this template, the template won't be instantiated due to SFINAE. Once the template is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1328 \textcolor{comment}{// instantiated it can look for global operator using normal conversions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1329 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define SFINAE\_OP(ret,op) decltype((void)(doctest::detail::declval<L>() op doctest::detail::declval<R>()),ret\{\})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1330 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1331 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DOCTEST\_DO\_BINARY\_EXPRESSION\_COMPARISON(op, op\_str, op\_macro)                              \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1333 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    DOCTEST\_NOINLINE SFINAE\_OP(Result,op) operator op(R\&\& rhs) \{                                   \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1334 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    bool res = op\_macro(doctest::detail::forward<const L>(lhs), doctest::detail::forward<R>(rhs)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1335 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(m\_at \& assertType::is\_false)                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1336 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            res = !res;                                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1337 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(!res || doctest::getContextOptions()-\/>success)                                          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1338 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            return Result(res, stringifyBinaryExpr(lhs, op\_str, rhs));                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1339 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        return Result(res);                                                                        \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1340 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1850 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1851         \textcolor{comment}{// kept here just for backwards-\/compatibility -\/ the comma operator should be preferred now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853         MessageBuilder\& operator<<(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& in) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} this-\/>operator,(in); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1855         \textcolor{comment}{// the `,` operator has the lowest operator precedence -\/ if `<<` is used by the user then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856         \textcolor{comment}{// the `,` operator will be called last which is not what we want and thus the `*` operator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1857         \textcolor{comment}{// is used first (has higher operator precedence compared to `<<`) so that we guarantee that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858         \textcolor{comment}{// an operator of the MessageBuilder class is called first before the rest of the parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1859         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}

\DoxyCodeLine{3364 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3365     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366     \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = T;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3368     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369     \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = std::atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3372 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS) || defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3373     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3374     \textcolor{keyword}{using }MultiLaneAtomic = Atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376     \textcolor{comment}{// Provides a multilane implementation of an atomic variable that supports add, sub, load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377     \textcolor{comment}{// store. Instead of using a single atomic variable, this splits up into multiple ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3378     \textcolor{comment}{// each sitting on a separate cache line. The goal is to provide a speedup when most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3379     \textcolor{comment}{// operations are modifying. It achieves this with two properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3380     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3381     \textcolor{comment}{// * Multiple atomics are used, so chance of congestion from the same atomic is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3382     \textcolor{comment}{// * Each atomic sits on a separate cache line, so false sharing is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3383     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3384     \textcolor{comment}{// The disadvantage is that there is a small overhead due to the use of TLS, and load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3385     \textcolor{comment}{// is slower because all atomics have to be accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3386     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3387     \textcolor{keyword}{class }MultiLaneAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3388     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3389         \textcolor{keyword}{struct }CacheLineAlignedAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3390         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3391             Atomic<T> atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3392             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(Atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394         CacheLineAlignedAtomic m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3396         \textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(CacheLineAlignedAtomic) == DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397                       \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}guarantee one atomic takes exactly one cache line"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3398 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3399     \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400         T operator++() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1) + 1; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3402         T operator++(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3404         T fetch\_add(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_add(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3406         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3407 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3408         T fetch\_sub(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3409             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_sub(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3412         \textcolor{keyword}{operator} T() \textcolor{keyword}{const} DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} load(); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3413 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3414         T load(std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) \textcolor{keyword}{const} DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415             \textcolor{keyword}{auto} result = T();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto} \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417                 result += c.atomic.load(order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3418             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3422         T operator=(T desired) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{comment}{// lgtm [cpp/assignment-\/does-\/not-\/return-\/this]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423             store(desired);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} desired;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3427         \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} store(T desired, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428             \textcolor{comment}{// first value becomes desired"{}, all others become 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430                 c.atomic.store(desired, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431                 desired = \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3435     \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436         \textcolor{comment}{// Each thread has a different atomic that it operates on. If more than NumLanes threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437         \textcolor{comment}{// use this, some will use the same atomic. So performance will degrade a bit, but still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438         \textcolor{comment}{// everything will work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440         \textcolor{comment}{// The logic here is a bit tricky. The call should be as fast as possible, so that there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441         \textcolor{comment}{// is minimal to no overhead in determining the correct atomic for the current thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443         \textcolor{comment}{// 1. A global static counter laneCounter counts continuously up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444         \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Each successive thread will use modulo operation of that counter so it gets an atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445         \textcolor{comment}{//    assigned in a round-\/robin fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446         \textcolor{comment}{// 3. This tlsLaneIdx is stored in the thread local data, so it is directly available with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447         \textcolor{comment}{//    little overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448         Atomic<T>\& myAtomic() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449             \textcolor{keyword}{static} Atomic<size\_t> laneCounter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450             DOCTEST\_THREAD\_LOCAL \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} tlsLaneIdx =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451                     laneCounter++ \% DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3453             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} m\_atomics[tlsLaneIdx].atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455     \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4057 \textcolor{keyword}{namespace }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4058     \textcolor{keyword}{using namespace }detail;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059     \textcolor{comment}{// matching of a string against a wildcard mask (case sensitivity configurable) taken from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060     \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1088/Wildcard-\/string-\/compare-\/globbing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} wildcmp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* wild, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4062         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* cp = str;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4063         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4065         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}((*str) \&\& (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild != *str) : (tolower(*wild) != tolower(*str))) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067                (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4071             str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4072         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4073 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4074         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(!*++wild) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4077                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4078                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4079                 mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4080                 cp = str + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4081             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild == *str) : (tolower(*wild) == tolower(*str))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4082                       (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4083                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4084                 str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4085             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4086                 wild = mp;   }
\DoxyCodeLine{4087                 str  = cp++; }
\DoxyCodeLine{4088             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4089         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4090 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4091         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4092             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4093         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4094         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} !*wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4095     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4097     \textcolor{comment}{// checks if the name matches any of the filters (and can be configured what to do when empty)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4098     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} matchesAny(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* name, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::vector<String>\& filters, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} matchEmpty,}
\DoxyCodeLine{4099         \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4100         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (filters.empty() \&\& matchEmpty)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4101             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4102         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& curr : filters)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4103             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (wildcmp(name, curr.c\_str(), caseSensitive))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4104                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4105         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4106     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4107 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4108     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} hash(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} b) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4109         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (a << 5) + b;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4112     \textcolor{comment}{// C string hash function (djb2) -\/ taken from http://www.cse.yorku.ca/\string~oz/hash.html}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4113     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} hash(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4114         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} hash = 5381;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4115         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4116         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((c = *str++))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4117             hash = ((hash << 5) + hash) + c; \textcolor{comment}{// hash * 33 + c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4118         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hash;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4119     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4612                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4613                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(reported == \textcolor{keyword}{false})}
\DoxyCodeLine{4614                         reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unhandled SEH exception caught"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4615                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4616                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4617                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4618                 execute = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4619             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4620             std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4621         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4622 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4623         \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} allocateAltStackMem() \{\}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4626         FatalConditionHandler() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4627             isSet = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4628             \textcolor{comment}{// 32k seems enough for doctest to handle stack overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4629             \textcolor{comment}{// but the value was found experimentally, so there is no strong guarantee}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4630             guaranteeSize = 32 * 1024;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4631             \textcolor{comment}{// Register an unhandled exception filter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4632             previousTop = SetUnhandledExceptionFilter(handleException);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4633             \textcolor{comment}{// Pass in guarantee size to be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4634             SetThreadStackGuarantee(\&guaranteeSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4635 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4636             \textcolor{comment}{// On Windows uncaught exceptions from another thread, exceptions from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4637             \textcolor{comment}{// destructors, or calls to std::terminate are not a SEH exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4638 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4639             \textcolor{comment}{// The terminal handler gets called when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4640             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4641             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4642             original\_terminate\_handler = std::get\_terminate();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4643             std::set\_terminate([]() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4644                 reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Terminate handler called"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4645                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4646                     DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4647                 std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE); \textcolor{comment}{// explicitly exit -\/ otherwise the SIGABRT handler may be called as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4648             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4649 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4650             \textcolor{comment}{// SIGABRT is raised when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4651             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4652             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4653             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an uncaught exception is thrown FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4654             prev\_sigabrt\_handler = std::signal(SIGABRT, [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} signal) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4655                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(signal == SIGABRT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4656                     reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SIGABRT -\/ Abort (abnormal termination) signal"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4657                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4658                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4659                     std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4660                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4661             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4663             \textcolor{comment}{// The following settings are taken from google test, and more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4664             \textcolor{comment}{// specifically from UnitTest::Run() inside of gtest.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4665 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4666             \textcolor{comment}{// the user does not want to see pop-\/up dialogs about crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4667             prev\_error\_mode\_1 = SetErrorMode(SEM\_FAILCRITICALERRORS | SEM\_NOALIGNMENTFAULTEXCEPT |}
\DoxyCodeLine{4668                                              SEM\_NOGPFAULTERRORBOX | SEM\_NOOPENFILEERRORBOX);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4669             \textcolor{comment}{// This forces the abort message to go to stderr in all circumstances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4670             prev\_error\_mode\_2 = \_set\_error\_mode(\_OUT\_TO\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4671             \textcolor{comment}{// In the debug version, Visual Studio pops up a separate dialog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4672             \textcolor{comment}{// offering a choice to debug the aborted program -\/ we want to disable that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4673             prev\_abort\_behavior = \_set\_abort\_behavior(0x0, \_WRITE\_ABORT\_MSG | \_CALL\_REPORTFAULT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4674             \textcolor{comment}{// In debug mode, the Windows CRT can crash with an assertion over invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4675             \textcolor{comment}{// input (e.g. passing an invalid file descriptor). The default handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4676             \textcolor{comment}{// for these assertions is to pop up a dialog and wait for user input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4677             \textcolor{comment}{// Instead ask the CRT to dump such assertions to stderr non-\/interactively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4678             prev\_report\_mode = \_CrtSetReportMode(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_FILE | \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_DEBUG);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4679             prev\_report\_file = \_CrtSetReportFile(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_FILE\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4680         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4681 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5078     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} trailingBytes(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5079         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5080             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5081         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5082         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5083             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5084         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5085         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5086             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5087         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5088         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5089     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5090 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5091     uint32\_t headerValue(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5092         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5093             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x1F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5094         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5095         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5096             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x0F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5097         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5098         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5099             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x07;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5100         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5101         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5102     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5103 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5104     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hexEscapeChar(std::ostream\& os, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5105         std::ios\_base::fmtflags f(os.flags());}
\DoxyCodeLine{5106         os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)x"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5107             << std::uppercase << std::hex << std::setfill(\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) << std::setw(2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5108             << \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5109         os.flags(f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5110     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5111 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5114     XmlEncode::XmlEncode( std::string \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& str, ForWhat forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{5115     :   m\_str( str ),}
\DoxyCodeLine{5116         m\_forWhat( forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{5117     \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5118 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5119     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} XmlEncode::encodeTo( std::ostream\& os )\textcolor{keyword}{ const }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5120         \textcolor{comment}{// Apostrophe escaping not necessary if we always use "{} to write attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5121         \textcolor{comment}{// (see: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5122 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5123         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}( std::size\_t idx = 0; idx < m\_str.size(); ++ idx ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5124             uchar c = m\_str[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5125             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5126             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'<'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&lt;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5127             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\&'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&amp;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5128 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5129             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'>'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5130                 \textcolor{comment}{// See: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5131                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx > 2 \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'} \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{5132                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&gt;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5133                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5134                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5135                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5136 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5137             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5138                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_forWhat == ForAttributes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5139                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&quot;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5140                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5141                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5142                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5143 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5144             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5145                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check for control characters and invalid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5146 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5147                 \textcolor{comment}{// Escape control characters in standard ascii}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5148                 \textcolor{comment}{// see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/404107/why-\/are-\/control-\/characters-\/illegal-\/in-\/xml-\/1-\/0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5149                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x09 || (c > 0x0D \&\& c < 0x20) || c == 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5150                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5151                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5152                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5153 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5154                 \textcolor{comment}{// Plain ASCII: Write it to stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5155                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5156                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5157                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5158                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5159 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5160                 \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/8 territory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5161                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check if the encoding is valid and if it is not, hex escape bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5162                 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: We do not check the exact decoded values for validity, only the encoding format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5163                 \textcolor{comment}{// First check that this bytes is a valid lead byte:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5164                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means that it is not encoded as 1111 1XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5165                 \textcolor{comment}{// Or as 10XX XXXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5166                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c <  0xC0 ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5167                     c >= 0xF8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5168                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5169                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5170                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5171 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5172                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} encBytes = trailingBytes(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5173                 \textcolor{comment}{// Are there enough bytes left to avoid accessing out-\/of-\/bounds memory?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5174                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx + encBytes -\/ 1 >= m\_str.size()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5175                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5176                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5177                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5178                 \textcolor{comment}{// The header is valid, check data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5179                 \textcolor{comment}{// The next encBytes bytes must together be a valid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5180                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means: bitpattern 10XX XXXX and the extracted value is sane (ish)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5181                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} valid = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5182                 uint32\_t value = headerValue(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5183                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 1; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5184                     uchar nc = m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5185                     valid \&= ((nc \& 0xC0) == 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5186                     value = (value << 6) | (nc \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5187                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5189                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (}
\DoxyCodeLine{5190                     \textcolor{comment}{// Wrong bit pattern of following bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5191                     (!valid) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5192                     \textcolor{comment}{// Overlong encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5193                     (value < 0x80) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5194                     (                 value < 0x800   \&\& encBytes > 2) || \textcolor{comment}{// removed "{}0x80 <= value \&\&"{} because redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5195                     (0x800 < value \&\& value < 0x10000 \&\& encBytes > 3) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5196                     \textcolor{comment}{// Encoded value out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5197                     (value >= 0x110000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5198                     ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5199                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5200                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5201                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5203                 \textcolor{comment}{// If we got here, this is in fact a valid(ish) utf-\/8 sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5204                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 0; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5205                     os << m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5206                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5207                 idx += encBytes -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5208                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5209             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5210         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5211     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5212 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5213     std::ostream\& operator << ( std::ostream\& os, XmlEncode \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& xmlEncode ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5214         xmlEncode.encodeTo( os );}
\DoxyCodeLine{5215         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} os;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5216     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5217 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6807             std::sort(testArray.begin(), testArray.end(), suiteOrderComparator);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6808         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(p-\/>order\_by.compare(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}name"{}}, \textcolor{keyword}{true}) == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6809             std::sort(testArray.begin(), testArray.end(), nameOrderComparator);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6810         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(p-\/>order\_by.compare(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}rand"{}}, \textcolor{keyword}{true}) == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6811             std::srand(p-\/>rand\_seed);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6812 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6813             \textcolor{comment}{// random\_shuffle implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6814             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} first = \&testArray[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6815             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} i = testArray.size() -\/ 1; i > 0; -\/-\/i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6816                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} idxToSwap = std::rand() \% (i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6817 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6818                 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} temp = first[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6819 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6820                 first[i]         = first[idxToSwap];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6821                 first[idxToSwap] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6822             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6823         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(p-\/>order\_by.compare(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}none"{}}, \textcolor{keyword}{true}) == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6824             \textcolor{comment}{// means no sorting -\/ beneficial for death tests which call into the executable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6825             \textcolor{comment}{// with a specific test case in mind -\/ we don't want to slow down the startup times}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6826         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6827     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6828 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6829     std::set<String> testSuitesPassingFilt;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6871 }
